data-show-use-buffer="true">  <div class="heading"> Description </div> <div class="show-more-content text-body" itemprop="description"> <div class="id-app-orig-desc">Ram cleaner users: this apps seems to &quot;kill my service&quot; so use ignore list or maybe remove the Ram cleaner or task killer otherwise my app will not work well.<br>If you like the app please consider rate with 5 stars.<br>&quot;THIS APP DONT REPLACE THE STOCK LOCKSCREEN&quot; and YOU DONT NEED ROOT<br>this app will not work for Long press power button since its hardware related.<br>&quot;Ideal for avoiding shut down the device in the pocket&quot;<br>Smart lockscreen protector will TRY to block the &quot;power menu option&quot; so you can avoid people turn off, mute,set to airplane your device from your lockscreen, Battery Friendly<br>even with pin or password a thief can power off easily without unlock the phone.<br>If You have a Security app like Cerberus to find your phone, you dont want people can turn off the device in a easy way.<br>This App Could work or could NOT work (working on 90% of devices),if the app its not working try modify Delay time if the app, this will give some time before closin power menu.<br>Root its not needed,its only if you want custom &quot;Power Menu&quot; with Reboot or Power off working.<br>NOTE: Airplane mode its not working on android jelly bean 4.2 because google change the seurity behavior.<br>if you have any doubts, bugs or feature request email me to <a href="mailto:n3zdroid@gmail.com">n3zdroid@gmail.com</a> before leave a bad feedback please<br>Uses the next Open Source software:<br>Android-ViewPagerIndicator and ActionBarSherlock<br>by: JakeWharton<br>Project home: <a href="https://www.google.com/url?q=https://www.google.com/url?q%3Dhttps://github.com/JakeWharton/Android-ViewPagerIndicator%26sa%3DD%26usg%3DAFQjCNEUubsnxjMEtzrqu1TORYvnUrf6Mw&amp;sa=D&amp;usg=AFQjCNEUmhPfYkjlc3TiMjwd0UEJQ5V69A" target="_blank">https://github.com/JakeWharton/Android-ViewPagerIndicator</a> <br><a href="https://www.google.com/url?q=https://www.google.com/url?q%3Dhttp://actionbarsherlock.com/%26sa%3DD%26usg%3DAFQjCNEi9VIsf8_97eH7brX6B1Rc2lW6xQ&amp;sa=D&amp;usg=AFQjCNGsLGP1qPULLmwRCuzPtJurH02ROw" target="_blank">http://actionbarsherlock.com/</a><br>Permission explained<br>android.permission.PREVENT_POWER_KEY and android.permission-group.HARDWARE_CONTROLS &lt;-- need for receive long power button event to show power menu<br>android.permission.INTERNET &lt;--ads<br>android.permission.ACCESS_NETWORK_STATE &lt;--ads<br>android.permission.WAKE_LOCK &lt;-- &quot;wake up&quot; to show custom menu (if its enabled)<br>android.permission.DISABLE_KEYGUARD &lt;-- disable lockscreen or keyguard to show custom menu <br>android.permission.WRITE_SETTINGS &lt;-- to put in airplane mode the device<br> android.permission.RECEIVE_BOOT_COMPLETED  &lt;--start the service on boot<br> android.permission.ACCESS_SUPERUSER &lt;-- SuperUser for &quot;reboot&quot; and &quot;power off&quot; in menu.</div>  <div class="show-more-end"></div> </div> <div> <button class="play-button show-more small"> Read more </button> <button class="play-button expand-close"> <div class="close-image"> </div> href="/store/apps/details?id=com.wordpress.chislonchow.deviceadminkeyguard" title="Lockscreen Policy">    Lockscreen Policy  <span class="paragraph-end"></span> </a> </h2>  <div class="subtitle-container">  <a class="subtitle" href="/store/apps/developer?id=Chislon+Chow" title="Chislon Chow">Chislon Chow</a>   <span class="price-container"> <span class="paragraph-end"></span>   <span class="apps is-price-tag buy-button-container" data-doc-fetch-skip-cache="0" data-doc-fetch-vouchers="0" data-docid="com.wordpress.chislonchow.deviceadminkeyguard"> <div class="pon" style="display:none">1</div> <button class="price buy">    <span class="display-price">Free</span>   </button>    </span>      </span> </div>  <div class="description">  Disable multiple 3rd party widgets on the lockscreen. Also removes lockscreen camera access on some devices.<p>★ Featured on Android Police, CNET, Droid-Life<p># Uninstall<br>First go to the app&#39;s left swipe-in menu by choosing &#39;Deactivate&#39;. Or uncheck the app from the &#39;Device Administrator&#39; list under &#39;Security&#39; in your &#39;Settings&#39; application. This allows you to uninstall. <p># Android 4.4+<br>Lockscreen Policy is at end-of-life and is no longer expected to work consistently across all devices, because of various changes in KitKat by Google and device manufacturers. Thanks for supporting Lockscreen Policy!<p>NOT USEFUL on Samsung TouchWiz devices. From version 1.3.2, the app will ask the user to uninstall when run.</p> Tip: Use a third-party SMS app to hide SMS on the lockscreen. Uncheck &#39;Multiple Widgets&#39; in &#39;Lock screen&#39; system setting to turn off 3rd party lockscreen widgets. <p>Disables the camera widget in stock Android (Nexus/GPE). Leave this setting in &#39;ON&#39; position if you do not have a lockscreen camera widget.<p># Android 4.2.x<br>Known issue under 4.2.2 with widgets disabled:<br>With widgets disabled, the default clock widget toggles between the bold and the non-bold hour clock every other unlock. <p>If your device is rooted, use clock hack to get the device to consistently show the non-bold hour clock. Sorry for the inconvenience, but I had no control over this. This issue is fixed in Android 4.3. <p>If you do not re-root your device after updating to Android 4.3, it is HIGHLY RECOMMENDED you undo the clock hack before proceeding, or you will have no way of restoring the stock digital clock widget on your device.<p># Usage<br>1) Run application<br>2) Make selections, and press activate<br>3) In the &#39;Activate device administrator&#39; screen, choose &#39;Activate&#39;<br>4) Turn off undesired features using the toggle switches. Changes are made instantly. Make sure your lockscreen is enabled to see the results.<p># Hide App Icon from Launcher<br>If you enable this feature, you can undo this by adding a desktop &#39;Shortcut&#39; (identified as a &#39;Widget&#39; on some Launcher) to reopen the app to revert.<p>#Clock Hack for Rooted devices: <br>For users running Google firmware, you can now disable the bold-hour lockscreen clock with &#39;Clock Hack&#39;, accessible via the action bar menu even with widgets disabled in the lockscreen. <p>To undo or revert this, simply rerun &#39;Clock Hack&#39;. You will additionally have to manually remove the clock widget and readd the desired one for changes to take effect if your lockscreen widgets are on. Note that this setting persists even if you deactivate or uninstall this application. (Can take a couple of screen locks/unlocks to take effect)<p>There are several downsides to using this hack. You will also lose access to the same widget from your homescreen. This alternate clock also will not launch the alarm app on click, nor does it display your world clocks. <p>On Android 4.3, to restore the bold hour clock widget, you may need to manually readd the widget by first removing the non-bold hour fallback clock widget. <p># Caveats when disabling widgets on Android 4.2<p>Enabling this will force the lockscreen to use a &#39;default fallback widget&#39;. On Google builds, the default is the stock DeskClock digital clock widget (with bold-hour style). This behavior cannot be changed. <p>The bold hour clock only affects official Google builds, and is part of Google&#39;s proprietary firmware.<p>The rooted method implements the following from XDA, <br>http://forum.xda-developers.com/showpost.php?p=34561693&amp;postcount=35<p>The music controls will still appear as a new page when active, even with the lockscreen policies in place. <p># Privacy<br>I do not collect any personal information with this completely free application.<p>No permissions other than device administrator required.<p># Additional Notes<p>Uses Stericson RootTools http://code.google.com/p/roottools/<p># Translations<br>Portuguese: Thiago Oliveira<br>Polish: Damian Krysa<br>German: Philip Weber</p></p></p></p></p></p></p></p></p></p></p></p></p></p></p></p></p></p></p></p></p></p></p> <span class="paragraph-end"></span> <a class="card-click-target" (My n1 was repaired coz of that :&lt; ) <p>&#39;Lock Screen App&#39; is a tiny app that can help you lock easily (without power button).<p>Features :<br>•Lock device with one touch <br> (Same effect as pressing the power button)<br>•Not a widget so it does not run as service in the background<br>•Auto-kill itself after locking to save your Battery &amp; Memory<br>•Tiny in size (&lt;100k)<p>Features (Donation Version Only):<br>•Little bit faster<br>•Lock by long-pressing search button   **not work on xpad/apad and device without search key**<br>•Get updates earlier<p>★★ Please buy the donation version to support the dev! ★★<br>(You could find it using &#39;View more applications&#39;/ the link in the app&#39;s settings page) <br>   <br>Thank you! :D<p><br>Notes:<br>======<p>@@Compatibility Issues@@<br>------------------------------------<p>1.New / Updated Moto devices may not be supported <p>Moto disallows lock screen in their OS updates, so it would not work on moto devices after updates and new device like Droid 3. I have reported it to moto, but they did not agree to fix! <p>2. administration function, you must deactivate device administration *BEFORE* uninstall to avoid error!<p>To do this:<br>•Go to &quot;Lock Screen Settings&quot; (in launcher) -&gt; &quot;Remove Device Administrator&quot;<br> ~See screenshots~<br>Alternatively, you may do it via<br>•Go to Settings -&gt; Location &amp; security (or Security) -&gt; Select device administrators -&gt; Uncheck this app.<p>After that, uninstall it in Play Store, in case of error during uninstall in Play Store, do it at Settings-&gt;Apps-&gt;Lock Screen--&gt;Uninstall<p><br>[To use other hardware keys to unlock class="subtitle-container">  <a class="subtitle" href="/store/apps/developer?id=MirageStack" title="MirageStack">MirageStack</a>   <span class="price-container"> <span class="paragraph-end"></span>   <span class="apps is-price-tag buy-button-container" data-doc-fetch-skip-cache="0" data-doc-fetch-vouchers="0" data-docid="com.miragestack.smart.phone.lock"> <div class="pon" intelligent lock screen by addictivetips.com ***<br>Are you worried about exposing your PIN and Pattern while you unlock your phone?<br>Here comes Smart Phone Lock for the rescue.<br>Smart Phone Lock will set the current phone time as your unlock PIN for the lock screen. It will change the PIN magically on every minute! So, each time you unlock the device, the PIN will vary and you need not worry about prying eyes around you. The best part is, you need not memorise anything to remember the PIN. The modifiers will allow you to enhance the security to the next level.<br>Modifiers :<br>1) Offset PIN - You can set a number (Positive/Negative) and that number will be added/Subtracted from the current time.<br>Lets say the time is 03:30 and the offset is +10, then the current unlock code will be 0340.<br>2) Reverse PIN - If you enable this modifier, then the PIN is reversed number of the current time.<br>Lets say the time is 03:50 and the PIN to unlock the lock screen is 0530.<br>Also, Smart Phone Lock provides Date PIN as an alternative way to change the PIN. If you use Date PIN , then the PIN to unlock your lock screen will be changed based on your phone date.<br>FAIL SAFE : If you forget the PIN , Don&#39;t worry.At any point of time, you can use your default PIN which you have entered during the app installation. Default PIN will act as backup code to unlock your phone. So, you can log in with default PIN. Even if you forget the default PIN, after entering 3 wrong default PIN , there is an option to get the default PIN through SMS to the registered phone number<br>You can also hide Smart Phone Lock app icon from the App list by selecting hide icon option under settings. If you hide the icon, it will be tough to find you are using Smart Phone Lock. You can launch the app by dialling/calling 1234 in the phone.<br>The application provides various options like :<br>1. Swipe to unlock - Optionally you can enable the swipe to unlock screen in the app settings.<br>2. Widget Support - Optionally you can add any widget to the swipe screen. So you can control your music player , see weather details or any statistics by adding appropriate widget to the swipe screen.<br>3. Uninstall protection - Optionally you can enable the uninstall protection, so that others can’t uninstall the application without proper authentication. You need to disable the uninstall protection before trying uninstall application.<br>4. Battery saving mode - This application is designed to consume very very less amount of battery. If you wish, you can enable the battery saving mode in the application settings to increase the battery life further.<p>The app is password protected, you can access the app only after entering the default pin which you have set during installation.<br>New Features:<br>* Support for 24 hour timePIN<br>* Option change your custom lock screen pictures<br>* In-app purchase to remove ads <br>* Hiding the application Icon from the app list<br>IMPORTANT NOTE : The application will not work on encrypted devices.<br>IF YOU CAN’T LOGIN WITH DEFAULT PIN ALSO, PLEASE RESTART YOUR PHONE AND TRY AGAIN. IF YOUR PHONE BATTERY IS NOT REMOVABLE THEN LONG PRESSING THE POWER BUTTON WILL FORCE RESTART THE PHONE.<br>IF YOU FACE ANY ISSUES WHILE UNLOCKING THE PHONE CONTACT US BY MAILING help@miragestack.com
